That night, the National Government held a temporary emergency meeting, where Wan and Bao gave separate reports. They discussed countermeasures with each other. Wan returned to Ping by plane this afternoon and immediately met with Zhang Xueliang to report on the situation of the Nanjing meeting. (Special telegram on the 24th)

(Beiping) Wan Fulin and Bao Wen returned to Ping this afternoon, escorted by Liu Haishan and Lin Sixian sent by Jiang. Wan said that he arrived in Beijing on the 23rd and met with Jiang, reporting on the situation of the Japanese army invading the Eastern Provinces. Jiang was extremely indignant at the atrocities of the Japanese army, believing that it was a matter of the survival of the Chinese nation. The central government should be responsible for handling it. Our country should unite and face the external threat. Individuals should have the determination to sacrifice themselves. The central government has determined the steps to be taken. Minister Wang said that the international community has expressed goodwill towards us and supports justice. China has appealed to the League of Nations. The people in the south are extremely agitated. I reported the Deputy Commander's views to Jiang, repeatedly stating that the Northeast will absolutely obey the central government in foreign affairs and all other matters. Zhang Ji and Cai Yuanpei went to Guangdong on the 23rd. Guangdong telegraphed, expressing unity against external threats. Hu Hanmin and Li Jishen will come out again to jointly shoulder the national crisis. (Special telegram on the 24th)

Wang Zhengting

Reports on the Progress of Negotiations 30

(Nanjing) Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting met with reporters this afternoon and reported (1) that the tense situation in the case of the Japanese army's atrocities in the Eastern Provinces in the past two days has been seen in various newspapers and will not be reported again. After this incident occurred, the Japanese side clearly violated the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty of the Washington Conference, believing that this move by the Japanese side violated world-recognized treaties or agreements. Therefore, the National Government has formally submitted a request to the League of Nations and all countries that have signed the Anti-War Pact, requesting that it be handled fairly in accordance with the League of Nations Covenant and the Anti-War Pact. After this case was submitted, the Administrative Council of the League of Nations formally resolved three points the day before yesterday, and the Chairman of the Council, Spanish Foreign Minister Lele, formally notified the Chinese government. The National Government has now telegraphed a reply to Lele, expressing acceptance of the resolutions of each case and stating that in this incident, the Chinese army did not occupy the other party's territory at all. All troop movements were also non-resistance actions under orders. It should be requested to continue to handle this matter. According to the League of Nations' handling of disputes between the two countries over the years, there are precedents to follow, one being Paraguay and Bolivia, two being Poland and Lithuania, and three being Greece and Bulgaria, all of which have been handled accordingly. The solution in each case is nothing more than (1) both sides stop military actions and return to their original defenses, (2) send personnel to investigate the situation, and (3) make a decision based on the investigation report. Now, our country's request to the Administrative Council of the League of Nations to continue to proceed is to ask it to implement the above two or three methods. (2) After Shenyang was forcibly occupied by the Japanese, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has made two emergency protests. Recently, it received reports that Jilin, Changchun, Andong, and other places were also forcibly occupied by the Japanese army. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs lodged a third emergency protest yesterday. (3) Ambassador Jiang Zuobin has arrived in Japan to take office. After Wang finished reporting, reporters asked: 1. If the Japanese still ignore the three protests that have been lodged against Japan, does the Ministry of Foreign Affairs have other more effective methods? Wang replied that protest is a legitimate diplomatic procedure. Now that this matter has been submitted to the League of Nations, it should be viewed in terms of how the League of Nations and the countries of the Anti-War Pact are proceeding. If the Japanese side does not accept the resolution of the League of Nations, the League of Nations will have a second and third step method, so this case can only be handled by the League of Nations at present and cannot be directly negotiated. The reporters also asked whether it was true that the Japanese army had a plan to automatically withdraw to the railway area. Wang replied that it has not been verified. 2. Was it a fact that Chongguang visited Finance Minister Song in Shanghai early on the 19th and Song said that the Dong Province incident could be negotiated directly between China and Japan? Wang replied that when Chongguang met Song, he did raise this idea. At that time, because the truth was not clear and it was thought to be a minor conflict, Song once said that it could be considered. A day or two later, he sent someone to inquire Song again. Song strictly refused, saying that this incident was not a minor conflict and of course could not be negotiated directly. 3. It is heard that the League of Nations will convene the Council again to discuss the China-Japan incident. Has the Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a report? Wang replied that there was a report, but the date was still unknown. (Special telegram on the 24th)

(Nanjing) Today, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stated that the rumor that the Ministry's reply to the international telegram contained a statement that it was a conflict between Chinese and Japanese troops, which reduced Japan's responsibility, was not true. (Special telegram on the 24th)

Japanese Conspiracy Exposed 31

Disguised Incitement of Riots

(Nanjing) A certain agency received a confidential report stating that the Japanese consulate in Jinan received a telegram from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of that country on the afternoon of the 21st, instructing it to hire more personnel and go to various places to collect various anti-Japanese slogans, and to incite workers in Shanghai, Qingdao, and other places to create an actual riot against Japan in the future to use as an excuse. On the evening of the 20th, a large number of military uniforms, collars, and identification badges of the Northeast Army and the Lu Army were sent from the Kwantung side, instructing the consuls in Jinan to distribute them to the Japanese merchants residing in the area in order to pretend to be our country's soldiers and create false evidence of killing Japanese and Korean residents. Furthermore, it secretly hired communist bandits from Shanghai to come to Jinan and Qingdao to carry out arson against Japanese residents to create an excuse for dispatching troops. Now, the central government has ordered the relevant local authorities to pay attention to this matter. (Special telegram on the 24th)

(Qingdao) The municipal government received a telegram from another port that people of a certain country are disguising themselves as our country's workers, inciting workers everywhere to carry out arson and looting, and creating incidents in order to create an excuse for dispatching troops. (Special telegram on the 24th)

The Japanese authorities also deny that various countries are aiding the Japanese army and claim that Japan will not increase the number of troops in Tianjin and has no intention of occupying Tianjin. However, a few days ago, the Japanese army was quite wary because the Chinese were angry, but it has calmed down recently. (Special telegram on the 24th)

San Francisco The Chinese Chamber of Commerce in San Francisco held a meeting today and passed a resolution requesting President Hoover to convene a China-Japan conference to consider the Manchurian issue. Only Humiliates Civilization 35

"The Chieftain's Nature of Disregarding the World Has Not Changed"

A Glimpse of American Public Opinion

New York The New York branch of the National News Agency compiled the opinions of major American newspapers today, all of which disapproved of the Japanese military's invasion in Manchuria. For example, the New York Morning Post said that although the Japanese wear modern European clothes, they have not changed their old habits. While Western countries are making every effort to help this once greatest country, Japan suddenly rose up to seize Shenyang by force. This kind of treacherous action that loses international trust has not completely washed away the chieftain's nature of the past. The New York World Telegram said that Japan's war against China violates the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Two years ago, the country had asked Soviet Russia to explain the reasons for invading Chinese land in northern Manchuria. Now Japan has committed the greatest crime of aggressive war in modern history. If the U.S. government is willing to protect its honor in the Kellogg Pact and the Washington Treaty, it should take action and immediately join the treaty countries to demand that Japan withdraw its troops and restore the original state. If necessary, it can come forward alone. The New York Lectures and Guidance Report said that there is now various evidence that can show that the Japanese atrocities in Manchuria were planned in advance by the leaders of the Japanese military. (Reuters telegram on the 23rd)

A Glimpse of Germany's Attitude 36

(Berlin) The semi-official Diplomatic Political Daily published an article. The attitude of the German authorities towards the Sino-Japanese dispute can be seen in it. The article stated that as far as the current situation in Manchuria is concerned, it cannot be called a war. At least one party must truly want to go to war before it can become a war. Now, both China and Japan clearly do not want to go to war. Although the Japanese army is flexing its muscles, it does not dare to offend the world and promote a war. The League of Nations should spare no effort to eliminate this unfortunate and dangerous conflict. The fate of the League of Nations itself is tied to Manchuria, because if it cannot fulfill its responsibility for this major event, its prestige will be swept away. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Yesterday, the Overseas Chinese all flew half-mast flags to show national humiliation. The conference decided to oppose Japan but not to riot. The proposal to boycott Japanese goods was unanimously passed. In order to protect the peace between the Chinese and Japanese in this area, the conference elected a number of important local Chinese to form a committee to advise the Overseas Chinese not to take violent actions against individual Japanese residents. A Glimpse of American Public Opinion

New York The New York branch of the National News Agency compiled the opinions of major American newspapers today, all of which disapproved of the Japanese military's invasion in Manchuria. For example, the New York Morning Post said that although the Japanese wear modern European clothes, they have not changed their old habits. While Western countries are making every effort to help this once greatest country, Japan suddenly rose up to seize Shenyang by force. This kind of treacherous action that loses international trust has not completely washed away the chieftain's nature of the past. The New York World Telegram said that Japan's war against China violates the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Two years ago, the country had asked Soviet Russia to explain the reasons for invading Chinese land in northern Manchuria. Now Japan has committed the greatest crime of aggressive war in modern history. If the U.S. government is willing to protect its honor in the Kellogg Pact and the Washington Treaty, it should take action and immediately join the treaty countries to demand that Japan withdraw its troops and restore the original state. If necessary, it can come forward alone. The New York Lectures and Guidance Report said that there is now various evidence that can show that the Japanese atrocities in Manchuria were planned in advance by the leaders of the Japanese military. (Reuters telegram on the 23rd)

(Hankou) Over the past few days, more than twenty Japanese warships have successively entered Hankou and anchored in the river off the Japanese concession. Frequent cannon fire suggests a show of force. All sectors are taking coordinated steps to avoid provoking the Japanese. (24th Dispatch)

Important Foreign News

Britain Accepts 69

The Suggestion to Halt Military Preparations

The Labour Party Issues a Political Program

Actively Preparing for the Election

London, 23rd Reuters - Baldwin stated in the House of Commons today that the government had issued an instruction to Lord Cecil, permitting him to accept the proposal by French Foreign Minister Briand for an immediate cessation of the arms program pending the proposals of the Disarmament Conference, but this would only be effective after other countries had accepted it uniformly. Baldwin also stated that he could declare that, barring unforeseen circumstances, the British government would not increase the army and air force expenditures for the 1932-33 fiscal year. According to a Geneva Reuters report, British representative Cecil reported at a League of Nations meeting today that Britain had accepted the French Foreign Minister's proposal and asked all countries to declare their opinions on this peace effort by November 1st. The ambassadors to Belgium and America have accepted the proposal for an immediate cessation of arms on behalf of the United States. The only countries that have not yet agreed are Japan and Poland. The Japanese representative argued that the matter should be discussed by the Disarmament Conference. The Polish representative said that Poland must obtain full guarantees from its neighboring countries.

London, 24th Reuters - According to general opinion, a general election will be held soon. The Labour Party is now preparing for an election contest. The Labour Party newspaper disclosed the Labour Party's election platform today: (1) Consistent opposition to tax rates, (2) Rebuilding industry and agriculture, (3) Abolishing indemnities and war debts, (4) Rapid implementation of disarmament, (5) Management of banks and finance. A Conservative Party newspaper predicted today that if a general election were held immediately, the Labour Party would lose 100 seats. The Liberal Party is now preparing everything. It is heard that the Liberal Party is unanimously opposed to socialism, and most of the party's members of parliament are prepared to recognize tax rates when necessary. Prime Minister MacDonald is recuperating in the countryside due to overwork. There should be new developments on this matter after his return to London.

Public Telegrams 70

Telegram from the Chinese Students Club of Wooster College to the Shen Bao: Please forward to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. World opinion is that negotiations should not be conducted directly with Japan.

Telegram from the Chinese Students Club of Washington to the Shen Bao: Please forward to the National Government. If justice is not upheld, we will fight Japan to the death.

Telegram from Paris to the Shen Bao and to all comrades from all sectors and parties of the country: Xiang Ning left the country two years ago, and her weak body can hardly support her. Hearing of the floods and tens of millions of disaster victims wandering and losing their homes, her heart is saddened and her eyes are full of tragedy. Who can surpass this extreme? All who have blood and conscience, who can be without feelings, how can they explain themselves? Recently, I also heard that Japanese imperialists have occupied Shenyang and Changchun. The Premier has long recognized the conspiracy of imperialism, so the reorganization in 1924 united small and weak nations to resist. In recent years, our party has disintegrated, and there have been frequent wars, causing the people to wither and be scattered. At this time of internal and external troubles, how can we delay and burn the beanstalk to cook the beans? How should we strive to make up for past mistakes, rescue the disaster victims, and jointly resist foreign aggression to save the country and party from the disaster of destruction? 何香凝 [He Xiangning's name].

Telegram from Luzhou to all newspaper offices: Our association has raised over a thousand yuan from various sectors in the local area and will remit it to the National Relief Committee in a few days. Special mention. The Hefei Sixth Middle School Flood Relief Association kowtows.

Telegram from Yangzhou to all newspaper offices: Recently, we read Deputy Commander Zhang Hao's telegram, stating that Japanese soldiers have been acting freely in Shenyang, occupying cities, expelling officials, severing communications, killing soldiers and civilians, and destroying our troops and arsenals. Upon hearing this news, our hearts are filled with anger. All who have blood should seek self-preservation. If we do not plan in time, it will be impossible to recover. Therefore, we offer three points to inform the people of the country: First, we should be determined to fight to the death. The Japanese soldiers are tyrannical and practice aggression. The reason for this is that our country has always advocated peace and retreated in the face of events, causing imperialism to gain an inch and want a yard, and to apply the methods used against the Korean people to our country on a double scale. The people of our country are on the brink of national extinction, and there is no reason to endure and not resist. Even a trapped beast will fight, let alone humans. We should resolutely adopt the principle of拼命主義 [pin ming zhu yi; risking one's life] and fight to the end. In the American War of Independence, did they have a pre-determined chance of winning at the beginning? They only succeeded because of the unity of all and the shared hatred of the enemy. Moreover, at this time, our army has organization, our government orders are systematic, and all equipment is far superior to that of America in the past. If we can all hold the determination to have either us or the enemy, what enemy cannot be pushed back, what fortress cannot be conquered? Our people, let us rise up and plan for it. Second, internal strife should be stopped quickly, and we should unite to resist foreign aggression. With internal bandits spreading and poisoning the lives of the people, although we have suppressed them painfully, they have not been fundamentally eliminated. In addition, there are natural disasters and unprecedented catastrophes. Everywhere is full of mourning and people are waiting to be fed. Anyone with a conscience knows that the vitality of the country has been greatly damaged, and we cannot make more bean-cooking incidents to hasten our demise. Therefore, the first priority for saving the country today is to pray that all comrades and compatriots immediately abandon their prejudices, eliminate internal strife, and unite to overcome the national crisis. Time is not waiting for us. If we delay, we fear we will be too late. Third, saving the country and resisting the enemy must rely on self-improvement, not just hoping for foreign aid. This time, the Japanese soldiers advanced into Shenyang, Changchun, Andong, and other places, brazenly violating the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Their barbarism and tyranny are incomprehensible. Not only are they bullying our country, but they are also disregarding justice and public law. Although various countries in the world may speak out for justice and uphold public law when they see this atrocity, if we do not improve ourselves, but want to rely entirely on the help of others and侥倖圖存 [jiao xing tu cun; hope to survive by luck], how can this be reasonable? Heaven helps those who help themselves. We should learn from the ancient precepts. The rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of everyone. We urge our compatriots to rise up and fight urgently to save us from today's crisis. Jiang and others have been in the army for decades and have received great favor from the country without repaying a single drop. Now that the great enemy is attacking horizontally and the country is pressed by disaster, we are willing to die in the front and fight to the death with the enemy to seek survival for the nation. We are armed and waiting for orders and will not hesitate to do our duty. We offer these pressing words and beg you to consider them. Zhang Zhijiang, Sun Lianzhong, Liang Guanying, Gao Shuxun, Guan Shuren, Dai Fanzhou, Zhang Zhankui, Zhang Huatang, Yang Tianbin, Wu Pengju, Zhao Ying, Li Songkun, Dong Zhentang, Ji Zhentong, Chi Fengcheng, Liu Guoming, Zheng Tingzhen, Wang Xiushen, Zhu Changde, Shi Dexue, together kowtow.

Bad news is spreading, and the whole country is in grief and anger. At this critical time of survival, how should all Chinese people rise up and be雄 [xiong; powerful]? News Highlights

Tianjin Reporter Group 71

Going to Liaoning for On-the-Spot Inspection

(Special Correspondent's Dispatch)

A Group of Nineteen People

News Heard Along the Way

It was reported that last night (the 18th), the Japanese army suddenly occupied Shenyang, cut off the BeiNing Railway, and guarded the transportation facilities. Only this morning at 6:00 AM did the Tianjin station of the BeiNing Railway Bureau receive a report. This shocking act, which violates international law, has spread throughout the city, causing widespread tension. Therefore, I decided to immediately go to Liaoning to investigate the truth. At 11:30 AM, I arrived at the East Station and saw seventeen reporters from various newspapers arriving, as if by agreement. There was also one reporter each from the English-language North China Star and the English-language Times, showing that Westerners are paying close attention to Japan's violent actions. On the platform, there were over a hundred Japanese people boarding a train to Tanggu, which was quite noticeable. After investigation, it was learned that they were returning to their country under orders from their government, preparing to organize a reserve army. As the train was about to depart, twenty or thirty Japanese women waved handkerchiefs and cheered, seemingly wishing them well on their return to the military. On the train, I met a certain official from the Railway Bureau, who said that at 10:00 PM last night, a company of the Japanese garrison stationed in Shenyang took a train from the South Manchuria Railway Station to HuangguTun (the site where Zhang Zuolin was assassinated in the 17th year of the Republic) and dismantled the tracks. Another unit of the Japanese army opened fire and attacked Beida Camp. Our Northeast Army endured in silence, not firing a single shot in return. The Japanese army occupied the commercial district, guarded transportation facilities to prevent the news from leaking, and attacked the Beida Camp arsenal and mortar factory. This was the situation before 5:00 AM this morning. However, this kind of action by the Japanese army had become an open secret five days ago. The Northeast authorities maintained a calm attitude. Until last night and this morning, the Japanese army bombarded Beida Camp with artillery. The extent of casualties and losses of our army is unknown, but it is known that the Second Division stationed in Liaoyang is rushing to Shenyang, arbitrarily harassing people along the way. It is also heard that the Japanese army occupied Yingkou last night and kidnapped Station Master Wang. At 4:00 PM, the train passed through Luanzhou. According to news from the station, the Japanese fleet anchored in Lushun received an emergency mobilization order last night and is expected to arrive in Tianjin tonight or tomorrow morning. According to general observation, the arrival of the Japanese fleet in Tianjin is merely a means of intimidation against us. Since Tianjin and Gugu are major ports in the north and the focus of international attention, they presumably dare not openly occupy them. However, as the Japanese army's arrogance is on the rise, there may be provocations against us in the future.

In the dining car, I also met Noguchi Norikiyo, a reporter from the Japanese Asahi Shimbun. He saw that we looked uneasy and asked whether our trip was voluntary or coerced, and whether the Municipal Party Department and the Deputy Commander's Headquarters were sending people. I told him that our trip was entirely voluntary and that there were no personnel from the Municipal Party Department or the Deputy Commander's Headquarters on this train. After the meal, I proposed organizing a group action. It was decided to form the News Reporter Shenyang Incident Investigation Group, and Panalulu, a reporter from the English-language Beijing-Tianjin Times, was elected as the group leader; Hu Shirong, a reporter from the North China Star, was elected as the English interpreter; Wang Jian, a reporter from the Yishi Daily, was elected as the Japanese interpreter.

Page 10

Page Three 72

Everyone will collect materials, compile them, and submit them to Xu Yin, the head of the BeiNing Railway's Public Relations Section, to send a public telegram to various newspapers in Beijing and Tianjin. Individuals are not allowed to send separate telegrams to avoid conflicting reports. Finally, Asahi reporter Noguchi expressed his willingness to introduce us to the Japanese Consul General in Liaoning, Hayashi Kyujiro, and the Commander of the South Manchuria Garrison Army, Honjo Shigeru, which was approved by the group. The names of the reporters are listed below: Zhu Xiaofu, Tianjin correspondent for the Shanghai Shen Bao; Xu Zhushi, Tianjin correspondent for the Xinwen Bao; Plante, China correspondent for the German Berliner Tageblatt; Wang Songnian, Tianjin correspondent for the Dagong Bao; Wang Tingshen and Wang Jian, reporters for the Yishi Daily; Deng Xizhang and Ni Huanzhang, reporters for the Yong Bao; Hu Shirong, reporter for the English-language North China Star; Li Yizan, reporter for the Shang Bao; Wang Zhuoyuan, reporter for the Minguo Daily; Yao Baolian, reporter for the Guowen News Agency; Panalulu, reporter for the English-language Beijing-Tianjin Times; Kleinert, Wittich, and Ma Shifu, reporters for the German-Chinese Daily; Zhang Chuzhen, reporter for the Guomin News Agency; Jin Huaixia, reporter for the Duowen News Agency; Yang Huinong, reporter for the Fudan News Agency; and nineteen others.

At 8:00 PM, the train passed through Qinhuangdao and Shanhaiguan. Armed Japanese soldiers patrolled the platforms with loaded guns, acting arrogantly. Upon inquiry, the stationmaster said that the long-distance telephone on this line can only reach Goubangzi, while telegrams can still reach HuangguTun. The situation in Shenyang is unclear, but Yingkou has indeed been occupied by the Japanese army. The city's police and training camps have been disarmed. Twelve miles away from Yingkou, the tracks have been destroyed, and landmines have been planted near Dawa Station. Railway employees have been kidnapped. At the same time, Haicheng has also been occupied. Yang, the chief of the Yingkou section, heard the news in Goubangzi and took train No. 106 to Beijing at noon to report to Director Gao Jiyi. (The above is news obtained from stations along the BeiNing Railway on the 19th, written on the train.)

After the train passed Suizhong, I lay down to sleep, but I couldn't fall asleep because my mind was too stimulated. At 0:30 AM on the 20th, we arrived in Jinzhou. Sun Aiting, a counselor from the Jilin Provincial Government, boarded the train to Liaoning. Sun is an old friend of mine, so I asked him about the situation in Shenyang. He said that the Japanese army began military action at 10:00 PM on the 18th, first destroying the Liukong Bridge between HuangguTun and Shenyang on the BeiNing Railway, and then firing shots into the air. Rong Zhen, Director of the Military Affairs Department of the Northeast Commander's Office, and Zang Shiyi, Chairman of the Provincial Government, immediately went to meet Consul General Hayashi, telling him that if there were any problems, they could be discussed. They asked who would be responsible for the nighttime shelling, which could cause misunderstandings. Hayashi replied that the shelling would stop in five minutes. Unexpectedly, Rong and Zang were detained and not released until 3:00 AM on the 19th, while the sound of artillery never stopped throughout the night. Shells landed on the ammunition depot of Beida Camp, causing an explosion. The Third Brigade of the Liaoning garrison, under Wang Yizhe, adopted a policy of non-resistance and never fired a single shot in return. A certain regimental commander was shot and wounded by the Japanese army, and there are rumors that Wang Yizhe was also killed. After the Japanese army began military action, they occupied the commercial district and attacked the city of Shenyang. Fearing a repeat of the Jinan May 3rd Incident, the local authorities immediately opened the city gates, and the Japanese army poured in, occupying the Northeast Commander's Office, the Deputy Commander's Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, the Provincial Government, the Telephone Bureau, the Telegraph Bureau, the Radio Station, and other institutions. They disarmed the guards and replaced them with Japanese soldiers, prohibiting people from leaving. After the Japanese army occupied the city of Shenyang, they divided their forces and exited the East Gate. One route attacked the Northeast Arsenal, and the other attacked the Jiangwutang Military Academy. The arsenal was occupied without resistance. The mortar factory, not having received orders from their superiors, refused to open its doors. The Japanese army immediately launched an attack. The guards inside the factory, for self-defense, initially returned fire, but after receiving orders from their superiors not to resist, they opened the factory gates. The Japanese soldiers then entered and carried out a massacre to vent their anger. The Northeast Jiangwutang Military Academy was also occupied without resistance. At the same time, the residences of various generals and leaders of various institutions were guarded by Japanese soldiers, allowing entry but not exit. Therefore, Director Rong and Zang Zhangxi lost their freedom of movement. The area east of the railway along HuangguTun is within the Japanese military's restricted zone. Vegetable vendors and merchants west of the railway can enter the restricted zone after inspection, but those within the restricted zone are not allowed to cross the railway to the west. Since the Japanese soldiers have cut off communication facilities and prohibited Chinese from leaving the restricted area, their intention is to prevent the leakage of their brutal actions. After 8:00 AM on the 19th, news from Shenyang was completely cut off, and the situation is unknown. One battalion of the Third Brigade stationed in HuangguTun, due to its isolation and weakness, took a train west at 8:30 AM and arrived in Jinzhou at 10:00 PM. At 8:40 AM, six Japanese soldiers took an electric handcar to XinminTun, four of them entering the Japanese Consulate, and the other two returning to HuangguTun. It is said that those who went to XinminTun were conveying the order of Japanese Army Commander Honjo, ordering the local veterans to assemble and await orders. Telegrams from Jilin, Changchun, and other places have also been completely cut off since 8:00 AM. Zhang Zuoxiang, Chairman of Jilin Province, returned to his ancestral home in Jinzhou due to his father's death. He has received a telegram from Deputy Commander Zhang, ordering that no matter how the Japanese army oppresses us, our army is not allowed to resist. At the same time, he ordered the 12th Brigade stationed in Jinzhou, under Zhang Jianxu, to move to the Shanhaiguan-Qinhuangdao area, which has already been dispatched. Sun was ordered by Zhang Zuoxiang to go to Shenyang to meet Consul General Hayashi and investigate the situation after the incident. The train stopped before reaching Goubangzi and was met by another train from XinminTun. According to people at the station, the situation in Shenyang is chaotic, and many of our soldiers, police, and civilians have been massacred by the Japanese army. (Written at Goubangzi Station at 4:30 AM on September 20th)

Central Government Announcement

Guidelines for Volunteer Army Education 74

The Central Executive Committee announced the Guidelines for Volunteer Army Education on the 24th. The full text is as follows: (Article 1) All schools above the senior high school level nationwide shall organize youth volunteer armies, and all schools at or below the junior high school level shall organize boy scout volunteer armies. Implement military training, swear to believe in the Three Principles of the People, wisdom, courage, loyalty, faith, wipe out humiliation, save the country, aid the government, and discipline: 1. Sacrifice oneself, love the Republic of China, and always be loyal and courageous citizens; 2. Obey orders and strictly abide by discipline; 3. Develop labor habits and practice group living; 4. Help others in need and serve the public at any time and any place; 5. Never use Japanese goods for life. (Article 2) All faculty and staff of schools nationwide shall take the same oath as the students and be earnestly responsible. In teaching and management, follow the following requirements: 1. Take the loyalty, courage, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace established by the Prime Minister as the moral guidelines, earnestly focus on the training of students' thoughts and personalities, and earnestly cooperate with students to create a whole group life. Pay attention to their own words and deeds as a model for students. (Article 3) All schools nationwide shall implement the following articles in the curriculum: 1. Pay attention to the history and geography of the country, especially the history of diplomacy and national defense geography; 2. For female students, pay attention to physical education, develop habits of hard work and endurance, and teach knowledge of wartime nursing and first aid; 3. In terms of training implementation, we must focus on promoting the national spirit and creating a strong and courageous style. All romantic, decadent, and decadent literature and art are absolutely prohibited; 4. Add courses on Japanese issues. (Article 4) Students should work hard in their studies and not strike. (Article 5) Students, in their time outside of class, must gather and work hard in accordance with the spirit of these education guidelines. (Article 6) Take diligence, struggle, wiping out humiliation, and saving the country as precepts. (Article 7) Schools nationwide should hold morning meetings every morning and shout the following slogans: Always be loyal and courageous citizens, wipe out China's national humiliation, restore China's territory, revitalize the Chinese nation, Long live the Three Principles of the People, Long live the Republic of China. (Article 8) These guidelines are formulated by the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and sent to the National Government for unified enforcement throughout the country.

Tense Anti-Japanese Work in All Circles After the County Party Department learned that Japanese soldiers had occupied Shenyang, it immediately led all circles to hold a mass anti-Japanese rally and established the All Circles Anti-Japanese Association. Yesterday (the 23rd), the committee held a meeting and resolved various items. Cai Zhongyu was allowed to resign as a committee member. Most of Zhang Mengxing was arrested. Zhang Yiyun, Lu Changlin, and Zhang Mengxing were elected as standing committee members. Jiading 76

A Brief Account of the Mass Meeting on Diplomacy with Japan People from all walks of life in this county are extremely indignant at the Japanese people's forcible occupation of our eastern provinces, burning, killing, and looting. At 9:00 AM on the 23rd, a mass meeting on diplomacy with Japan was held at the public sports field. More than 2,000 people from all walks of life attended. On the spot, it was resolved to send two telegrams: one requesting the central government to make a decisive decision, implement revolutionary diplomacy, and recover all Japanese rights in China; and one requesting the whole country to unite against Japan and work together to save the country. They shouted anti-Japanese and national salvation slogans, organized a team to parade, and gave speeches separately inside and outside the city.

Suzhou 77

Merchant Corps to be Reorganized into Volunteer Corps There are seventeen branches of the Suzhou Merchant Corps, with more than 500 members. However, due to the name, they have not been trained for a long time. The corps now intends to reorganize the merchant corps into a business community volunteer corps, call up old members, and recruit new members for active training, as a backup to diplomacy. All store employees with five or more people must send one person. The implementation method is to convene an emergency meeting of the heads of each branch on the 27th to discuss everything.

County Budget Re-Tightened and Compiled The Wu County government has received instructions from the Finance Department to recompile the county budget for the 20th year of the Republic due to the water disaster and reduced autumn harvest. The original budget must be reduced by one-third. Yesterday (24th), the county government convened a meeting of representatives from various agencies and groups to discuss the matter, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The local income for this year is assumed to be 70%, and the expenditure should be reduced by 30%; (2) Organize a review committee to review it, and the review will begin on October 1st; (3) Administrative expenses should be tightened as much as possible; (4) Please have the party fees reduced by the party department itself; (5) Unnecessary projects will be held until the 21st year.

University and Middle School Students Publicize Anti-Japanese Activities Students from Soochow University and No. 1 Middle School divided into fifty teams on the 24th to publicize anti-Japanese activities in various places inside and outside the city, including five teams of female students, with twenty people in each team, speaking and weeping from house to house. They also scheduled to go to the countryside on the 26th to continue the publicity. Also, seven students from Xizhong arrived in Suzhou on the 24th, and fifty teachers from Huangdai Township also came to the city to give speeches.

New Drama Actor Swallows Opium to End Life Qian Banxiao from Jiangyin, 20 years old, studied at Soochow Attached Elementary School and then served in the 3rd Division of the National Army. He then switched to acting in new dramas and currently lives at No. 20 Shiquan Street in Suzhou. Due to the oppression of the environment and feeling the brutality of the Japanese army, he used the alias Duohun at 4:00 PM on the 23rd and swallowed three letters of opium at No. 2 Ankang Inn outside Changmen to commit suicide. He was discovered by the tea room and sent to Xujiang Hospital for treatment and recovered.

Wuxi 78

Chamber of Commerce Cables the Central Government to Announce Diplomatic Policy Yesterday, the County Chamber of Commerce cabled the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government, stating, "The Northeast Incident is imminent, with only aggression and no resistance. Is it true that our people are brave in private fights but timid in public battles? Not only can we not protect our territory, but we cannot even maintain our dignity. Please quickly determine the policy and announce it to the people, and telegraph border officials to strictly enforce precautions, carefully protect the territory, and avoid further negligence, in order to maintain the people's hearts."

Red Bandits Wang Jun and Others Executed by Firing Squad Four well-known Red bandits from Xiyi, Wang Jun, You Shengbao, Cao Hequan, and Xu Haizhou, were captured in Zhang Village in the Fifth District during the term of former County Magistrate Sun last year. After being sent to the county, the jurisdiction of the trial has been changed many times, so no verdict has been reached to this day. The Provincial Government recently decided that it should be handled by the Military Law Review Office of Jiangsu Province. After a trial, they were found guilty, and yesterday, the Military Law Review Office of Jiangsu Province signed the papers for the four criminals, verified their identities, and executed them by firing squad outside Zhenjiang.

The Investigation of the Li Gongshi Case Concluded The case of Li Zhilin, a villager from Yangshuyuan Township in the 16th District, who caused a sensation at one time, was investigated by the inspectorate, Xuanfang, of the Wu County District Court, who came to Xiyi to steam and examine the bones and verify the marks. The murderer, Li Zhilin, was brought to court for questioning and detained. It is now learned that the case has been concluded by Prosecutor Du, who determined that Li Zhilin (aka Alin) caused harm to people, resulting in death, and abandoned the body in an attempt to destroy the evidence, violating Articles 296 and 262, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. In accordance with Article 74 of the same law, he should be punished for the most serious crime. Except for the part of Zheng Aiquan et al. who damaged the property, which is dismissed separately, the public prosecution was brought to the Criminal Court of the same court yesterday in accordance with Article 253, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, awaiting review and judgment.

Changzhou 79

The Enthusiastic Anti-Japanese National Salvation Mass Meeting All circles in Wuyi held a meeting at the public stadium this morning (24th) at 9:00 AM. All shops were closed for half a day, and all factories sounded their whistles for five minutes when the meeting started. Representatives from various agencies, groups, schools, and the masses numbered no less than tens of thousands of people. The County Party Department, the County Government, the military police, and the regiment served as the presidium of the meeting. The atmosphere at the meeting was unusually tense. It was resolved to (1) telegraph the Central Government to issue a general mobilization order for the army, navy, and air force to prepare for war against Japan; (1) telegraph the Central Government to order all university and middle school students nationwide to implement emergency military training to prepare for war against Japan; (1) telegraph the comrades in Guangdong to cease fighting and unite against foreign enemies to save the country. Finally, they shouted slogans and paraded throughout the city with flags until noon before dispersing.

Shen Boxian was appointed to succeed him. Shen arrived in Zhenjiang yesterday afternoon and went to the Provincial Government to meet with Chairman Ye to discuss everything. His words were full of tears, and the whole audience was moved. As a result, the Jiangdu People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association was organized, and Wu Zunyi, Wang Jingting, and six others were elected as members. One hundred men formed a volunteer army, and seven men were appointed to draft the general outline of the volunteer army, scheduled for 10:00 AM on the 25th. A mass anti-Japanese national salvation meeting will be held, and a telegram will be sent to the whole country, calling for (1) domestic peace; (2) the implementation of national diplomacy; (3) the preservation of Manchu and Mongolian territory.

Correspondence

Letter from the Kunshan County Field Tax Collection Office 83

To the editor, I recently read a news item in the local correspondence column of your newspaper on the 20th of this month, entitled "A Shocking Case of Embezzlement of National Taxes." After reading it, I was shocked. Although our office gives receipts to the business owners first and exchanges them for grain certificates in the following year due to procedural reasons, there has never been a situation where taxes have been paid without grain certificates being given. Moreover, since the business owners are given grain certificates in the following year, how can there be grain certificates listed as civil debts after the exemption? Since there are no grain certificates listed as civil debts, how can such a large sum of money be embezzled? This is self-evident. Since the order was received in the 16th year of the Republic to handle all civil debts from the 4th year to the 15th year, our office immediately collected all the uncompleted grain certificates, compiled a list, and reported it to the Finance Bureau, which was clearly supervised and turned over to the Provincial Department for verification. It has been several years since then, and suddenly this news item was discovered. It is clearly a fabrication, intended to confuse the public, put people in an embarrassing position, and attempt to extort money. Because the matter is important, I have written to your newspaper in particular, hoping that it will be corrected. I am grateful for this. Respectfully, the Kunshan County Field Tax Collection Office, September 23rd.

Ministry of Education Guidance 84

Student National Salvation Movement

丨Seven Key Points Defined丨Telegram Order to Education Authorities

Intensify Military Training in Extracurricular Lectures

Do Not Strike and Focus on Physical Education Courses

Nanjing, 24th Central Telegram, In order to guide the student national salvation movement, the Ministry of Education telegraphed national universities and education departments in various provinces and cities on the 23rd, stipulating the key points: (1) Intensify the study of Japan's recent atrocities and its policy of aggression, with teachers in the school giving lectures or inviting scholars from outside the school to take charge; (2) Students may organize lecture teams to give lectures outside of class; (3) When students participate in various gatherings, faculty members should be responsible for leadership; (4) Intensify military training and focus on physical education courses; (5) Students should work hard in their studies and not strike; (6) Students should encourage each other to be diligent and hard-working, and vigorously avoid romantic and indulgent pleasures; (7) All actions of students should follow the instructions of the Central Government and abide by the laws and regulations promulgated by the Central Government and the government.

Nanjing, 24th Telegram, Central Committee members Dai Chuanxian, Chen Bulei, Fang Juehui, and Zhu Jiahua held a review meeting at the Central Party Headquarters at 5:00 PM today to review the student patriotic movement plan.

Universities Telegraphically Request Declaration of Policy

(9) The school authorities are requested to add nursing courses for female students to organize rescue teams when necessary. (10) All students in each school are ordered to raise national salvation funds to assist the government. (11) Efforts will be made to inspect Japanese goods. (12) Representatives will be sent to participate in the citizens' assembly on the 26th of this month. All of the above cases will be handled separately by the executive committee.

Executive Committee Meeting: The executive committee organized by the association is scheduled to hold its first executive committee meeting tomorrow at 2:00 PM, still at the Youth Propaganda Corps.

Executive Committee of the University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association 89

Shanghai-Hong Kong Interport Tennis 98

Hong Kong Team's Lun Keung Not Coming Due to Illness

Shanghai Team's Lin Qiu May Not Be Able to Attend

| Balance of Power Between the Two Sides May Be Affected |

The Shanghai-Hong Kong interport tennis match is scheduled to be held in early October. The Hong Kong team is scheduled to travel north on the Hoover President on the 29th of this month.

Damage to Hong Kong Team's Strength: The Hong Kong team's lineup initially included Lun Keung, the strongest player on the island. Now, however, due to heart enlargement pain, he has stopped coming to Shanghai. Doctors have instructed him to rest for at least three weeks. The Hong Kong team's strength has been greatly damaged as a result. The current lineup has been changed to Lo Man-wai (captain), Fenn, He Jialiu, and Ye Jun four people. The women's team will come along, and is quite strong, being Mrs. Tottenham, Ms. Lo and four others.

Hong Kong Team's Organization: The Hong Kong team will be organized with Fenn as the first singles player. Fenn and Lo Man-wai will be paired in one doubles match. The other two singles matches will likely be Lo Man-wai and He Jialiu. The women's team is likely to be unbeatable by Shanghai.

Lin Qiu May Not Attend: Lun Keung's absence has affected the Hong Kong team, but it is also feared that Lin Lang and De Fu of the Shanghai team will also be unable to attend. It is said that the regulations stipulate that representatives must reside in their representative area for at least one year. Therefore, the Shanghai team may be represented by Hyakuseki Yu, Canavero, and Wheat. The strength of both sides may therefore be more balanced.

Free Talk

Heartfelt Words 101

— Du Juan

Dear compatriots, what day is today? Are you still joyfully celebrating the Mid-Autumn Festival and eating mooncakes? When you take a round mooncake in your hand, you should think that our Republic of China was originally also round, like this mooncake. When you put it in your mouth to eat, you should think that the brutal sun (Japan) is treating our country like you eating this mooncake. The three northeastern provinces have been occupied, like a big corner bitten off the mooncake. Then, bite by bite, the mooncake will be eaten up, and our Republic of China will be finished. Alas, pitiful motherland, why are you fated like a mooncake?

Buchaotingcao Zhaifu Talks

Fake Good People 102

When Yan Xizhai was sixteen years old, his adoptive grandfather, Zhu Weng, wanted to bribe someone to get him a Xiucai degree. He cried so much that he refused to eat, saying, "I would rather be a true commoner than a fake scholar." We should all have this kind of spirit. One day, I was on the tram, carrying only two double coins (shuang jiaozi). I took them out to buy a ticket, but the ticket seller said, "Copper coins are no good." I had to get off and walk. Fake coins cause so much trouble, how much more fake people? Fake coins cannot be used, but fake people can get by. Why is that? True villains are easy to know, but hypocrites are hard to guard against. They look real but also somewhat fake; they sound fake but also somewhat real. Truth mixed with falsehood, and falsehood resembling truth. It confuses people, making it impossible to distinguish. How difficult it is to be in a fake society! Last summer, I wrote ten short poems about fake good people, with the intention of advising the world and encouraging myself. The wording may be excessive, but with sincere enthusiasm, I hope everyone will reform and create a bright and upright true world together. Forgive me or condemn me, let the people judge.

(1) Fake Good People

Why is the world so bad?

Bad because of fake good people.

Saying one thing but meaning another:

Though they are people, they are not!

(2) Fake Father and Son

Fake father and son!

Money is the father.

Calling "Papa" with their mouths,

Cursing him to die in their hearts.

(3) Fake Mother and Daughter

Fake mother and daughter,

Raising a daughter like raising a pig.

Whoever has more money,

Can buy the fat pig.

(4) Fake Husband and Wife

Fake husband and wife,

Appearing harmonious but their hearts are apart.

The wife sleeps with another man;

The husband visits prostitutes.

(5) Fake Lovers

Fake lovers,

Becoming strangers once they let go of hands.

Meeting a new stranger,

They become the one they desire again.

(6) Fake Friends

Fake friends,

Friendship is meat and wine.

Once the wine and meat are gone,

They spread your shame everywhere.

(7) Fake Teachers and Students

Fake teachers and students,

Transactions are in the books.

Once they want to overthrow each other,

It's only because of fewer points.

(Points are the grades you get)

(8) Fake Army

Fake army,

Watching the country fall apart.

They have their own skills:

Killing their own sisters.

(9) Fake Officials

Fake officials,

Mouths full of principles.

Eating the people's food,

Wanting to peel the people's skin.

(10) New Wu Song

I am the new Wu Song,

Already on Jingyang Ridge.

Meeting a man-faced tiger,

Beating it without negotiation.

Lament for the Three Northeastern Provinces 103

— He Tianjian

Duke Xiang of Song valued benevolence and brought about his own demise. Why do men wear military uniforms? Sleeping soundly by the bedside for so long, one night, the dove occupied the nest so arrogantly. Last night, the north wind opened the door, and 100,000 Japanese devils swept in. The artillery bombardment was fierce, and thunderbolts struck the sky. Shenyang, Jilin, and Changchun fell one after another, and Huanggu and Xinmin were repeatedly destroyed. How much is left of the three northeastern provinces? The killing and burning continue unabated. Princes were killed and officials were slaughtered, how cruel to these sons of Heaven. Turning back to the Northeast, murderous intent rises. The strong prey on the weak, who pities them? There is no justice in this world, justice depends on military strength. Alas, justice depends on military strength.

From September 19th of this year, Tianjian has withdrawn from the China-Japan Art Comrades Association. I do not wish to be informed of any future actions of the association, and I hope the association will no longer contact me by letter. Everyone has their own ambitions, let us not interfere with each other.

Anecdotes of Ding Ruchang 104

— Qing Qu

During the Sino-Japanese War, Liu Gong Island, a small place with black bullets, was held against the Japanese army. When ammunition and supplies were exhausted, the situation became critical. He wanted to seek a way out of certain death, hoping that victory would benefit the country and defeat would only harm himself. He called himself unyielding, and was truly worthy of praise. He eventually reached a point where there was no advance or retreat, no different from the defeat of the Nine Jiedushi at Xiangzhou. He died with his ambition unfulfilled, and was also burdened with a bad name, with no way to defend himself. Such was Ding Ruchang. When the Japanese army occupied Liu Gong Island, the remains of Ding Ruchang were carried onto the Kangji Wheel by the Japanese, who even fired cannons in salute, showing great respect. The spirit of loyalty and courage touches people, even enemies are no different. But when the hearse returned south, not only were those who saw it sneering, but even pointing fingers and calling him a traitor who lost the army and disgraced the country. This shows the national sentiment at the time. However, Ding, because his soldiers did not obey orders, committed suicide by taking poison, sacrificing himself. After his death, the soldiers began to surrender. This means that the intention to surrender must not have come from the Commander of the Navy. This is very clear. Alas, in times of peace, they enjoy high salaries, but when things get urgent, they are like in a dream and cannot save the situation, even surrendering the army to the enemy. Compared to Ding's death, those who willingly sacrifice themselves, how can the difference be measured?

When Ding was committing suicide, he was still cursing a certain high official. Because his telegram requesting battle had just been sent, he received a hand-written order forbidding him to send troops and not to leave Weihai for even one step. If he violated it, he would be punished even if he won. This constraint led to his being trapped by the enemy and eventually defeated. At that time, there was the Beiyang Minister and the Naval Yamen. Their powers were mixed and did not benefit the situation. A scholar told Jin Wuzhu, "With powerful ministers inside, no general can achieve merit outside." I say the same about Ding. The Sino-Japanese War was nearly forty years ago, and the cunning of our eastern neighbor is even worse than before. In the face of foreign aggression, I recall the events of Lord Ding, also to encourage those who take up arms for the country.

Chain of Happiness in National Crisis 105

— Ms. Ye Hua

The Japanese took advantage of our natural disaster to launch a military campaign, forcibly occupying our territory, burning and killing our soldiers and civilians, trampling on our institutions, and detaining and humiliating our officials. The shocking news spread, making people's eyes split and their hair stand on end. Our five internal organs were destroyed and torn apart. The whole country was in shock and anger, extremely sad. Every descendant of the Yellow Emperor wants to wash away this shame. A certain gentleman from the Shanghai Municipal Government, heartbroken, created a new Chain of Happiness and sent it to friends, hoping to encourage them and show his determination to endure hardship and bide his time. I will record the words below, hoping that all readers of the newspaper will work together. The words say: "The brutal Japanese, taking advantage of our country's natural and man-made disasters, disregarding justice, brazenly sent troops and forcibly occupied our important ports such as Shenyang and Changchun. Wherever their iron hooves go, the rivers and mountains change color. Alas, the compatriots of the Northeast have become slaves of a lost country. At this critical moment, at this moment of national life and death, we should struggle together, holding the following resolutions: (1) Never buy Japanese goods.

(2) Adhere to the principle of non-cooperation.

(3) Strive to fulfill the duties of a citizen, be loyal and diligent, serve society, and dedicate ourselves to the country.

(4) Practice the Premier's teachings: "Loyalty, Filial Piety, Benevolence, Love, Faith, Righteousness, Harmony, and Peace."

(5) Sweep away selfish desires and make national welfare and people's interests the premise of everything.

Please, after receiving this letter, no matter how busy you are, copy ten copies within twenty-four hours and send them to your closest friends and relatives. Guarantee that you will have a life of abundance, happiness everywhere, and eternal peace. Many children and grandchildren. Otherwise, great disaster will befall you, your family will be destroyed, you will be left without descendants, and you will live in a human hell.

Records of Things Seen and Heard in the Former Capital 107

— Zhu An

The Underlay Money

The Comprehensive Mirror for Aid in Government. In the Tang Zhenyuan thirteenth year, eunuchs used palace markets to buy things, still asking for tribute door and foot money. Hu notes. Tribute door refers to the fact that all doors passed by the tribute have expenses, like the guiding fee during the reign of Emperor Ling of Han. In the old days, officials inside and outside the capital used openers. (commonly known as door people) The Bunjia asked for bribery from those who wanted to see them. The most evil habit was called the door package. Even the palace was no exception, and it was even worse. Looking at this, it has been a long time. Most of the door people are northerners. Every time the capital is simplified, they interact and solicit. The poles are woven like looms. They all hope to follow, regarding it as a source of profit. Even if there are people of integrity who want to ban it, they will say that we rely on this for a living. Otherwise, who would be willing to travel thousands of miles to follow us? The situation is like this. There is nothing to be done. Those who love themselves only strictly order these people not to extort. Foreign officials are fine. Beijing officials are especially poor. What their family depends on is only the disciples and old officials who come to see them. Knocking on the door and gifting them with a few gold coins. However, they can never rely on their power to demand as foreign officials can. In addition to the door package, the underlay money is the big source. The underlay money is that when the owner buys something, they ask to keep 2% of the price when paying the money to lubricate the family. This is the common practice that has been followed. If there are exceptional demands, there will be no end. Therefore, buying things from the store must be more expensive than the servants buying them. This is because the store has prepared a place in advance. This is also what the Tang people called the door, under the Beijing officials. This is where the greedy maggots gather. The official so the officialdom is not clear, and the capital is ruined. These people have lost their reliance. However, the custom of underlay money cannot be changed. In recent years, however, the cleaning money for renting a house has no longer been seen. The cleaning money is that every time a lease is made, the landlord and the tenant's servants each get one month's rent and divide it. The tea money is called three shares. The tea money is that the first month of renting a house must pay an extra month's rent as a deposit. When the contract is terminated, you can live for one more month without paying rent. This is because there are fewer residents every day, and the landlord has to demote himself. Otherwise, no one will ask about it. Looking at this, the atmosphere of the old capital will gradually become simple and simple. The old customs will eventually become relics.

Those with blood and qi, who would not regard it as an irreconcilable enemy? How should we think of our great rivers and mountains, about to fall under the iron hooves of the Japanese? How should we think of the current national crisis of our nation, with life at stake, and cut ourselves to the bone, bursting out hot blood? But things are not like that. At this moment of life and death, under the watchful eyes of tigers and wolves, the people of the country seem to forget the danger of their own situation, and still indulge in the joys of singing and dancing, regarding compatriots as grass and the country as worn-out shoes. I really don't know what they are thinking. And I don't know where they will die. "The singing girl does not know the hatred of a lost country, and still sings the Backyard Flower across the river." This can be sung for such people.

Driven by the whip of life, Yi, in addition to serving in a company during the day, still works as an accountant in a certain dance hall at night. Since the bad news was announced, I thought the dance hall would close itself without closing its doors. But unexpectedly, the decadent music just came out of the hands of the musicians, rippling in the intoxicating square hall, filled with confusing gazes, and shot out from the eyes of the charming dancers, twinkling in the dim light. Those who were attracted by these two things and came one after another, except for a few foreigners, most of them were still countrymen. Their extravagance in opening champagne and the way they were intimate with the dancers, their high spirits, were no less than on the eve of the Japanese massacre in the three northeastern provinces. Didn't they know about the large-scale Japanese invasion? It's almost unbelievable. But when they hug Japanese dancers in their arms, they often use this matter as a source of teasing, as if it were the ultimate sweet talk. And the Japanese dancers answer with their intoxicating voices, saying, "This is a national event. It has nothing to do with us. Let's enjoy ourselves. The music is playing again. Our people are originally friendly. Don't disturb our peace with this matter. Why don't we dance?" They laugh loudly when they hear this, and then hug each other on the smooth board, implementing their principle of Sino-Japanese friendship and enjoying themselves. Are they completely without conscience? Why are they so insane? It is strange.

Shuobu Rotary Club

A Husband's Wife (23) 108

— Jiang Hongjiao

"Your view is wrong. A wife should only be responsible for managing the household herself. It's difficult if the husband insists that she must manage the household. For example, if a wife doesn't have the experience and ability to manage the household, you can't blame her for not managing it. I think a wife who can't manage the household has the self-awareness to simply not manage it, which is better than not being able to manage the household but insisting on managing it, making things worse. I ask myself that I am willing to manage the household, and I am also able to manage the household, but he dislikes me for interfering too much and not managing it well. I also want to simply not manage it. If there is a suitable job, I can find one. I really want to go out to work. I think it is extremely dangerous for a woman to not earn money herself and only rely on her husband. Can you pay attention to me and introduce me to a job?"

"I know your ability. It must be possible to find something that pays a few dozen yuan a month. But there are only two people in your family. If you go out again, there will really be no one to manage the household. If Mr. Li finds out that I introduced you out, he will definitely hate me."

"He is your friend, and I am also your friend. Why do you only care about him and not help me at all?"

"I can sacrifice my friendship with Mr. Li, but if people find out, it may cause a lot of trouble."

"Hey! I dare not ask you anymore. But you have already heard about his and your wife's whereabouts, and there are also many rumors outside. Isn't this the trouble that has arisen?"

"What did you hear? Tell me!"

"I will declare one thing first. I am definitely not jealous. I only hope that your couple will not have an extra gap because of my husband's relationship, or even have a major resentment. At the same time, I also hope that my husband will not have such a close relationship with any woman. So, I am only alone at home. I hide all my depression in my own stomach. There is no one to talk to. If I don't go out to find a job to relax, I will get sick from being depressed."

"I will also be honest with you. I put everything about her out of my mind and don't ask anything. To put it more bluntly, even if she really has some ambiguity with your husband, I will let her do it. I am very optimistic about everything and don't think it's a big deal. I only ask my own conscience not to be sorry for people. It is very difficult to find a job outside now. Don't say women, even men, ask for help from all aspects, but it is still useless, let alone women. If you really want to go out to work and are not afraid of others gossiping, then I am also prepared to ignore anything and think of a way for you. My company is thinking of adding a clerk. You can definitely take on the job. The monthly salary is at least fifty yuan and at most seventy or eighty yuan. Can you go?"

"I will definitely go. What day can I go to contact?"

"I will talk to the manager tomorrow, and it will probably be successful."

Their long conversation lasted more than three hours before it ended, because Mrs. Li had to prepare dinner. She made several delicious dishes herself and ate with Chen Xian at a table, just like a family.

Current State of the Financial World Yesterday 114

In the several days since the Japanese army occupied our Eastern Provinces, the financial world, influenced by the prevailing environment, has experienced an extraordinary credit crunch, a sudden change in public bonds, and an increasingly tense atmosphere in the market. In terms of foreign exchange, various banks have been frantically seeking foreign currency to serve as reserves for banknotes, causing the exchange rate to continue to rise. Fortunately, those in charge have been making every effort to maintain stability. As for the credit situation, it was initially caused by Japanese merchants withdrawing cash. Subsequently, it was reported that merchants from Changchun, Qingdao, Shenyang, Liaoning, and other regions, whose ancestral lands had been ravaged by the Japanese army and whose vitality had been severely damaged, would have difficulty repaying their debts to the financial world in Shanghai. This further alarmed the financial world, leading to a very dangerous situation in the preceding days. By yesterday, although the overnight lending rate still appeared to be above 4%, the actual situation had eased. It is said that merchants from various regions, upon seeing reports of tight credit in Shanghai, have been collectively remitting large sums of money to Shanghai, with telegraphic transfers, mail transfers, and cash arriving in an endless stream. Furthermore, banks along the Bund, in order to maintain the market, are also reportedly providing as much collateralized lending as possible. While the truth of this cannot be guaranteed, it is undoubtedly good news for financial panic. However, according to those in charge of the financial world, although the Shanghai financial market may experience temporary changes, these will not last long. From a broader perspective, a solution is expected within a few days that will restore the market to its normal state.

Stock Market 115

Presenting an Unprecedented Spectacle

Four Bonds Continued to Fall to the Limit and Halt Trading in the Morning

Ten Bonds Soared to the Limit and Halt Trading in the Afternoon

Fluctuations of Seven or Eight Yuan Caused Extreme Confusion

Yesterday's stock exchange, due to the delay in collecting supplementary margins, did not begin trading until after 11:00 a.m., resulting in only one trading session. Futures trading was extremely active, and bond prices continued to fluctuate significantly. The market was filled with buying, and the tense situation showed no sign of easing. Futures for September delivery of the 1919 Customs Bonds, Consolidated Tax Bonds, and Salt Tax Bonds all reportedly continued to fall to the limit and halt trading. The strong-weak divergence between the current month and next month's futures was a particularly unique phenomenon in the current stock market. This is because most holders of goods are eager to sell their current month's futures in order to raise cash, while speculators on the long side are also aware that the end-of-month delivery is imminent, and if they do not quickly seek to sell, they will inevitably have to take delivery. This has led to a short squeeze. Those who are unable or unwilling to take delivery are unanimously selling, resulting in a supply-demand imbalance, with the September futures trading two, three, or even four yuan lower than the October futures, reversing the usual situation of bond prices being higher in the near term and lower in the long term. In the afternoon, the exchange urgently discussed ways to stabilize the market, delaying the opening of trading. Brokers temporarily engaged in off-market trading, with few transactions and prices slightly lower than in the morning session. Trading resumed at 6:00 p.m., and the market situation suddenly changed dramatically. News spread that the diplomatic situation had taken a turn for the better, with the United States accepting the League of Nations' notification and formally expressing its position to intervene in the Japanese army's atrocities in Northeast China and demand their withdrawal from our country. Furthermore, the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and other major banks, in order to stabilize the market, have responded to the exchange's request to continue buying and engaging in arbitrage transactions. They have also allowed bonds to be used as collateral in response to market needs, boosting investor confidence. This led to a new record in the unprecedented fluctuation of bond prices, as buying surged and various bonds rebounded and halted trading. The four bonds that had fallen to the limit and halted trading in the morning were allowed to resume trading by the exchange for the sake of market safety and after collecting additional margins from short sellers. Their prices also rose sharply. Therefore, the net result of the day's ups and downs was a significant fluctuation of seven or eight yuan. Those who profited smiled, while those who lost shook their heads. The suddenness of the change was truly rare. There were still no spot transactions. The total value of futures transactions was 35.5 million yuan.

Nantou - There was not much supply yesterday. There were very few people at the market in the morning due to the rain.
